## Glossary
Here is the common terminology & abbreviation for the space sector with the EN‚ÄëRU conversions. There are almost no abbreviations for [organizations](contact.md), payload & terms within a single project. Marks:

   - An approximate number of EN‚ÄëRU terms: **1‚ÄØ174** √ó 2. *(Note. How to count = a number of lines ‚àí 49 ‚àí 27√ó9)*
   - ‚âà terms are partial equivalents, use with caution;
   - ‚Üî just literal translation with no matches.
